# Data dictionary for the 2010 census tract-level files provided by `{censoBR}`


## Description

This file documents the content of the census tract-level aggregate files made available by the R package `{censoBR}` for the **2010 Demographic Census**. For more info on the package, check the [official GitHub page](https://ipeagit.github.io/censobr/). 

All census tract-level aggregate files were downloaded by the script `code/01-download-data.r`, which saves the datasets in parquet format in the `data/raw` folder with names in the format `2010_*.parquet`.

When available, the dictionary incorporates metadata from the Markdown transcription of the original IBGE dictionary, stored in  `docs/2010_dictionary_tracts.md`.

When metadata are not available in that file, this is explicitly indicated.

This data dictionary was generated by Pedro H. G. Ferreira de Souza, with support from OpenAI Codex using GPT-5.5.

- Generated on: 2026-04-25
- Total documented files: 8



## Companion CSV Structure

The content of this data dictionary is mirrored in the companion file `docs/data_dictionaries/2010_censobr_data_dictionary_eng.csv`.

This CSV file contains one row for each variable in each parquet file related to the census tract-level aggregates from the 2010 Census. That is, the combination of the `file_raw` and `column_name` columns provides unique identifiers for each row of the CSV file.

The CSV file contains the following columns:

- `file_raw`: exact name of the parquet file to which the row refers, such as `2010_Pessoa.parquet`.
- `dataset_name`: short name of the dataset derived from the file, such as `Pessoa`, `Basico`, or `Entorno`.
- `column_name`: exact name of the column as it appears in the parquet file.
- `column_order`: position of the column in the parquet schema, indexed from 1.
- `type_parquet`: data type of the column in the parquet file, such as `string` or `double`.
- `source_sheet`: source file, block, or documentation section used as the metadata source when available.
- `source_name_original`: original name or code of the variable in the source documentation, such as `Cod_setor`, `V1005`, or `V001`.
- `theme`: thematic grouping of the variable in the documentation.
- `label_pt`: short Portuguese label of the variable, used as the main description in the dictionary.
- `categories`: categories or value labels when the documentation provides that information; blank when no categories are associated.
- `coverage_notes`: note about the universe of tracts and the coverage of the file to which the column belongs.
- `key_role`: functional role of the column in the dataset, such as `primary_key`, `geo_id`, `descriptor`, or `measure`.
- `join_key`: indicates whether the column can be used as a join key, with values such as `yes`, `no`, or `possible`.
- `present_in_workbook_dict`: kept for compatibility with the 2022 dictionary; for 2010, it receives `not_applicable` because the metadata source used here is the Markdown derived from the original PDF.
- `present_in_md_dict`: indicates whether the variable is documented, for that specific file, in the source Markdown dictionary or in its geographic identification section.
- `notes`: free-text field for observations, caveats, name differences, reused metadata, inferences, or specific documentation issues.

Columns standardized by `{censoBR}`, such as `code_tract`, `code_muni`, `code_state`, and `code_region`, were linked to the original names described in the Markdown when there was an explicit match. Columns without a direct match, such as `code_weighting`, were kept in the dictionary with inferred metadata and `present_in_md_dict = no`.



## Overview of Parquet Files

| File                           | Dataset            | Rows | Unique tracts | Duplicates | Columns | Documented in Markdown? |
| --------------------------------- | ------------------ | -----: | -------------: | ---------: | ------: | ------------------------ |
| 2010_Basico.parquet               | Basico             | 310120 |         310120 |          0 |      35 | yes                      |
| 2010_Domicilio.parquet            | Domicilio          | 310120 |         310120 |          0 |     383 | yes                      |
| 2010_DomicilioRenda.parquet       | DomicilioRenda     | 310120 |         310120 |          0 |      23 | yes                      |
| 2010_Entorno.parquet              | Entorno            | 310120 |         310120 |          0 |    1169 | yes                      |
| 2010_Pessoa.parquet               | Pessoa             | 310114 |         310114 |          0 |    2008 | yes                      |
| 2010_PessoaRenda.parquet          | PessoaRenda        | 310120 |         310120 |          0 |     141 | yes                      |
| 2010_Responsavel.parquet          | Responsavel        | 310114 |         310114 |          0 |     334 | yes                      |
| 2010_ResponsavelRenda.parquet     | ResponsavelRenda   | 310120 |         310120 |          0 |     141 | yes                      |

**Notes:**

- The files are in `data/raw/`.
- The `Unique tracts` and `Duplicates` columns use the `code_tract` variable as reference.
- The `Documented in Markdown?` column indicates whether metadata exist in `docs/2010_dictionary_tracts.md` for at least part of the file.
